# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Collar
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Neck
- Color: Red
- Stat Buffs
    - Luck ✦ = 9
    - HP ✦ = Lx2.5
    - Attack Plus = L
    - Damage Plus ✦ = Lx1.25
    - Power = D+1
- Actives:
    - [Lighten Target](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Lighten+Target)
    - [Flaming Gaze](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Flaming+Gaze)
    - You have access to Tiers I-IV of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Ydilikian (Medieval)
